<rate>1</rate>< Review>
I had my first encounter with Meineke when I bought a car from one of the Smog Technicians at the store for $1200. Turns out it was one of those 'buy back' deals the government does, where they give you $500 for a clunker to junk it so you have some new cash for a new car to buy; but the guy just turned around, pulled the check engine light out, and sold it to me. Among other problems I have, I'm physically disabled, so that right at the bat is pure taking advantage of.

For years I avoided Meineke, telling them that the place was haunted with terrible people.   But today I was extremely ill, my day off, and the only place I know in Fallbrook that does oil Change is Meineke, my father had been saying "naw, they have new owners, just go check it out, that guy that stole from you isn't there anymore blah blah blah" so I was like fine, their oil changes are $50 but screw it, rather not drive to WalMart when I'm feeling so ill, almost hospital ill, just stop by Meineke. I have a bad feeling about these places, so I check under my hood, the hoses, breaks, etc. to make sure they have no stupid sales pitch to give me. Everything fine, a little bit of dirt, but hoses and clamps are all nicely places, belts fresh, and I'm expecting 'you need tires' deal.

I walked in, wanted oil change, made it clear I've never heard of 'extra special oil' and did not accept the upsale. I sat outside. Five minutes into the oil change, guy comes out, and I think hes straight up joking with me, "Your radiator is leaking."

Me: "No its no, aha."
Him: "Yes it is, its leaking."
Me: "You gotta be kidding, I just looked at it five minutes ago and it was just fine. I've done mechanic work before."
Him: "I'll show you."

I said, no that wasn't there before, it was 100% fine five minutes ago, and they must have done something to it, and I'm not going to pay for something they broke, and I want to leave. So either by random statistical anomaly never before happened in the history of the world, my radiator happened to by itself go out in the five minutes between me driving it to the shop (because I had manually check myself) and the fifteen seconds of driving it from the garage to their parking area.

"We are all trying to make money here."
"If you drive off, your engine will blow, do don't want that, do you?"
"What do you mean, you don't have enough money, you have enough money to get your wheels back, don't you?"

I mean, this was straight up extortion. I saw the guy deliberately damage my car, the other mechanics backed him up in bullying me, meanwhile, I need medication and my child is with me, my day off, the only day I have to do things, waiting for these horrible sociopathic people to let me go.  They didn't. I was really close to calling the cops.  I didn't know what to do.

Apparently, someone in my family called and offered to pay for the repair. I don't know what type of swindling went on, but there was definitely some total criminal bad juju going on here.

DO NOT GO HERE. IF THEY BELIEVE YOU CANNOT FINANCIALLY SUE THEM OR FIND ANOTHER MODE OF TRANSPORTATION THEY WILL EXTORT YOU.

< review>
If you are looking to use Makespace, think again -- consider other more reliable options. Makespace truly was storage without a struggle, up until pick up. Post the pickup, it went downhill....

My appointment was about a month ago, but I still have not gotten any confirmation from the team about my things in storage (supposed to take 3 days or so). When I reached out to CS after week 2 , they said 4 of my items are still being processed and "they don't know why." They said they reached out to ops to process, but I'm still waiting. Although they were kind, CS just made me worry more, because they sounded clueless themselves --didn't seem like they had the info they need to help. I was also told  "there was very little I can do for the unprocessed items."

What am I supposed to do? Just hope that I can get my stuff back some day?

Cherry on top --  based on the photos of my items currently posted by Makespace, it should be more than 4 items that still need to be processed. Alas, it's hard to tell, because the team packed a bunch of things in their own box without labeling what is inside...I tried to ask my CS rep to help me find out what's inside, to no avail.

They closed their support phone lines, so I can't reach anyone in person. A few days ago I expressed my concern that I'm worried my stuff is missing & asked if something is going on at the warehouse ...no response.

I get that their demand is crazy due to COVID. People at the company must be stressed. If that is the case and so things are just hectic and there are significant issues, Makespace should have just let me & other customers know so at least we can wait in peace while hopefully they figure things out. It's really frustrating having to spend so much time & mindshare to ensure a storage company, well, actually stored my things. I'm just glad I didn't store any important documents.

The movers who showed up were truly fantastic though --showed up on time, super polite, got my things out of my apartment really fast. My rep who assisted up to my pickup, was also great. I'm sad to be leaving such a bad review.</review>
